Good point.

To help others, it makes most sense to only discuss one issue at a time. I.e. just one of two apparmor denied messages per thread. And two threads for example. Using good titles. Keeping search engines in mind, so people having the same issue easily landing here. A good title for example looks to me:

Patrick March 20, 2015, 4:29pm #6

We dont have a flood of activity yet in this forum. And deterring posts by complicated rules seems wrong at this point. At some point we might need to switch to a pragmatic, have rules + ignore the not-so-well written bug reports + work on well written bug reports approach due to lack of time.

In my signature are some links (HOT: How to Ask Smart Questions | How to Report Bugs Effectively) that are supposed to explain how to write very good reports.
